trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Trading bot class to manage API connection and execute the trading strategy.
'''
from ibapi.client import EClient
from ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper
from ibapi.contract import Contract
from ibapi.order import Order
import threading
from utils import calculate_momentum, log_trade
class TradingBot(EClient, EWrapper):
    def __init__(self):
        EClient.__init__(self, self)
        self.next_order_id = None
        self.market_data = []
        super().connect("127.0.0.1", 7497, clientId=1)  # Use the inherited connect method
        thread = threading.Thread(target=self.run)
        thread.start()
    def disconnect(self):
        # Disconnect from the API
        self.done = True
        super().disconnect()
    def nextValidId(self, orderId):
        # Callback for the next valid order ID
        self.next_order_id = orderId
    def get_market_data(self):
        # Subscribe to market data for a specific contract
        contract = self.create_contract()
        self.reqMktData(1, contract, "", False, False, [])
    def tickPrice(self, reqId, tickType, price, attrib):
        # Callback to handle incoming market data
        if tickType == 4:  # Last price
            # Store or process the price data as needed
            self.market_data.append(price)
            print(f"Market data received: {price}")
    def execute_momentum_strategy(self):
        # Implement the momentum trading strategy
        self.get_market_data()
        momentum_signal = calculate_momentum(self.market_data)
        if momentum_signal:
            contract = self.create_contract()
            order = self.create_order()
            self.place_order(contract, order)
    def create_contract(self):
        # Define contract details
        contract = Contract()
        contract.symbol = "AAPL"
        contract.secType = "STK"
        contract.exchange = "SMART"
        contract.currency = "USD"
        return contract
    def create_order(self):
        # Define order details
        order = Order()
        order.action = "BUY"
        order.orderType = "MKT"
        order.totalQuantity = 10
        return order
    def place_order(self, contract, order):
        # Place an order based on strategy signals
        if self.next_order_id is not None:
            self.placeOrder(self.next_order_id, contract, order)
            self.next_order_id += 1
            log_trade({"contract": contract, "order": order})
    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):
        # Handle errors
        print(f"Error: {reqId} {errorCode} {errorString}")
```

'''
GUI interface for user interaction with the trading bot.

import tkinter as tk
from trading_bot import TradingBot
class TradingBotGUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Trading Bot")
        self.bot = TradingBot()
    def setup_gui(self):
        # Set up the GUI components
        start_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Start Trading", command=self.start_trading)
        start_button.pack()
        self.root.mainloop()
    def update_display(self):
        # Update the GUI with current data and status
        # Placeholder for updating display logic
        pass
    def start_trading(self):
        # Start the trading process from the GUI
        self.bot.execute_momentum_strategy()

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data processing and strategy implementation.
'''
import numpy as np
def calculate_momentum(data):
    '''
    Calculate momentum indicators for the strategy using RSI.
    '''
    if len(data) < 14:
        return False  # Not enough data to calculate RSI
    # Calculate RSI
    gains = [data[i] - data[i - 1] for i in range(1, len(data)) if data[i] > data[i - 1]]
    losses = [-data[i] + data[i - 1] for i in range(1, len(data)) if data[i] < data[i - 1]]
    average_gain = np.mean(gains[-14:])
    average_loss = np.mean(losses[-14:])
    if average_loss == 0:
        return True  # Simplified signal when no losses
    rs = average_gain / average_loss
    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
    # Example condition for momentum signal
    if rsi > 70:
        return True  # Overbought condition
    elif rsi < 30:
        return False  # Oversold condition
    return False
def log_trade(trade_details):
    '''
    Log trade details for forward testing and analysis.
    '''
    # Placeholder for logging trade details
    print(f"Trade logged: {trade_details}")

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Trading bot class to manage API connection and execute the trading strategy.
'''
from ibapi.client import EClient
from ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper
from ibapi.contract import Contract
from ibapi.order import Order
import threading
from utils import calculate_momentum, log_trade
class TradingBot(EClient, EWrapper):
    def __init__(self):
        EClient.__init__(self, self)
        self.next_order_id = None
        self.market_data = []
        super().connect("127.0.0.1", 7497, clientId=1)  # Use the inherited connect method
        thread = threading.Thread(target=self.run)
        thread.start()
    def disconnect(self):
        # Disconnect from the API
        self.done = True
        super().disconnect()
    def nextValidId(self, orderId):
        # Callback for the next valid order ID
        self.next_order_id = orderId
    def get_market_data(self):
        # Subscribe to market data for a specific contract
        contract = self.create_contract()
        self.reqMktData(1, contract, "", False, False, [])
    def tickPrice(self, reqId, tickType, price, attrib):
        # Callback to handle incoming market data
        if tickType == 4:  # Last price
            # Store or process the price data as needed
            self.market_data.append(price)
            print(f"Market data received: {price}")
    def execute_momentum_strategy(self):
        # Implement the momentum trading strategy
        self.get_market_data()
        momentum_signal = calculate_momentum(self.market_data)
        if momentum_signal:
            contract = self.create_contract()
            order = self.create_order()
            self.place_order(contract, order)
    def create_contract(self):
        # Define contract details
        contract = Contract()
        contract.symbol = "AAPL"
        contract.secType = "STK"
        contract.exchange = "SMART"
        contract.currency = "USD"
        return contract
    def create_order(self):
        # Define order details
        order = Order()
        order.action = "BUY"
        order.orderType = "MKT"
        order.totalQuantity = 10
        return order
    def place_order(self, contract, order):
        # Place an order based on strategy signals
        if self.next_order_id is not None:
            self.placeOrder(self.next_order_id, contract, order)
            self.next_order_id += 1
            log_trade({"contract": contract, "order": order})
    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):
        # Handle errors
        print(f"Error: {reqId} {errorCode} {errorString}")
```

'''

import tkinter as tk
from trading_bot import TradingBot
class TradingBotGUI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Trading Bot")
        self.bot = TradingBot()
    def setup_gui(self):
        # Set up the GUI components
        start_button = tk.Button(self.root, text="Start Trading", command=self.start_trading)
        start_button.pack()
        self.root.mainloop()
    def update_display(self):
        # Update the GUI with current data and status
        # Placeholder for updating display logic
        pass
    def start_trading(self):
        # Start the trading process from the GUI
        self.bot.execute_momentum_strategy()

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data processing and strategy implementation.
'''
import numpy as np
def calculate_momentum(data):
    '''
    Calculate momentum indicators for the strategy using RSI.
    '''
    if len(data) < 14:
        return False  # Not enough data to calculate RSI
    # Calculate RSI
    gains = [data[i] - data[i - 1] for i in range(1, len(data)) if data[i] > data[i - 1]]
    losses = [-data[i] + data[i - 1] for i in range(1, len(data)) if data[i] < data[i - 1]]
    average_gain = np.mean(gains[-14:])
    average_loss = np.mean(losses[-14:])
    if average_loss == 0:
        return True  # Simplified signal when no losses
    rs = average_gain / average_loss
    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
    # Example condition for momentum signal
    if rsi > 70:
        return True  # Overbought condition
    elif rsi < 30:
        return False  # Oversold condition
    return False
def log_trade(trade_details):
    '''
    Log trade details for forward testing and analysis.
    '''
    # Placeholder for logging trade details
    print(f"Trade logged: {trade_details}")

# Trading Bot User Manual

Welcome to the Trading Bot application, designed to execute a momentum trading strategy using the IBKR TWS API. This manual provides detailed instructions on how to install, configure, and use the software effectively.

## Introduction

The Trading Bot is a Python-based application that connects to the Interactive Brokers Trader Workstation (TWS) API to execute trades based on a momentum strategy. It includes a graphical user interface (GUI) for user interaction and supports forward testing of trading strategies.

### Main Functions

1. **Momentum Trading Strategy**: The bot uses the Relative Strength Index (RSI) to identify overbought and oversold conditions and execute trades accordingly.
2. **GUI Interface**: A simple interface built with Tkinter allows users to start the trading process and interact with the bot.
3. **Forward Testing**: The bot logs trade details for analysis and testing of the strategy's performance over time.

## Installation

### Environment Setup

To run the Trading Bot, you need to have Python installed on your system. The required dependencies are listed in the `requirements.txt` file. Follow the steps below to set up your environment:

1. **Install Python**: Ensure Python is installed on your system. You can download it from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

2. **Install Dependencies**: Use pip to install the necessary packages. Run the following command in your terminal:

   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

   This will install the `ibapi` library for API connection and `numpy` for data processing.

## Usage

### Running the Application

1. **Start the IBKR TWS**: Ensure that the Interactive Brokers Trader Workstation is running and configured to allow API connections.

2. **Run the Main Application**: Execute the `main.py` file to start the Trading Bot application. Use the following command:

   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

   This will launch the GUI interface.

### Using the GUI

- **Start Trading**: Click the "Start Trading" button in the GUI to initiate the momentum trading strategy. The bot will begin subscribing to market data and executing trades based on the strategy signals.

### Forward Testing and Analysis

- **Trade Logging**: The bot logs trade details for each executed order. This information can be used for forward testing and analyzing the strategy's performance.

## Documentation

For further information on the API and trading strategy implementation, refer to the following resources:

- **IBKR API Documentation**: [Interactive Brokers API Guide](https://interactivebrokers.github.io/tws-api/)
- **Momentum Trading Strategy**: Research articles and tutorials on RSI-based momentum strategies.

## Support

For any issues or questions regarding the Trading Bot application, please contact our support team at support@chatdev.com.

Thank you for choosing our Trading Bot application. We hope it enhances your trading experience and helps you achieve your financial goals.
